Option Explicit

' UserForm縲掲rmMacroSplash縲阪・譌｢螳壹げ繝ｭ繝ｼ繝舌Ν繧､繝ｳ繧ｹ繧ｿ繝ｳ繧ｹ・・B_PredeclaredId・峨↓萓晏ｭ倥＠縺ｪ縺・・' 謇倶ｽ懈･ｭ縺ｧ霑ｽ蜉縺励◆ UserForm 縺ｯ莠句燕螳｣險 ID 縺檎┌蜉ｹ縺ｫ縺ｪ繧翫掲rmMacroSplash 縺梧悴螳夂ｾｩ縲阪↓縺ｪ繧九％縺ｨ縺後≠繧九◆繧√¨ew 縺ｧ遒ｺ菫昴☆繧九・Private m_frmMacroSplash As frmMacroSplash

Private Function MacroSplash_Form() As frmMacroSplash
    If m_frmMacroSplash Is Nothing Then
        Set m_frmMacroSplash = New frmMacroSplash
    End If
    Set MacroSplash_Form = m_frmMacroSplash
End Function

Public Function MacroSplash_GetTxtExecutionLogScreenRectPixels(ByRef outL As Long, ByRef outT As Long, ByRef outW As Long, ByRef outH As Long) As Boolean
#If VBA7 Then
    Dim hwndSplash As LongPtr
    Dim hdc As LongPtr
#Else
    Dim hwndSplash As Long
    Dim hdc As Long
#End If
    Dim pt As POINTAPI
    Dim dpiX As Long
    Dim dpiY As Long
    Dim tb As Object
    On Error GoTo Fail
    MacroSplash_GetTxtExecutionLogScreenRectPixels = False
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Function
    hwndSplash = FindWindow(0&, SPLASH_FORM_WINDOW_TITLE)
    If hwndSplash = 0 Then Exit Function
    Set tb = MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog")
    If tb Is Nothing Then Exit Function
    dpiX = 96
    dpiY = 96
    hdc = GetDC(hwndSplash)
    If hdc <> 0 Then
        dpiX = GetDeviceCaps(hdc, LOGPIXELSX)
        dpiY = GetDeviceCaps(hdc, LOGPIXELSY)
        Call ReleaseDC(hwndSplash, hdc)
    End If
    pt.x = 0
    pt.y = 0
    Call ClientToScreen(hwndSplash, pt)
    outL = pt.x + CLng((CDbl(tb.Left) * dpiX) / 72#)
    outT = pt.y + CLng((CDbl(tb.Top) * dpiY) / 72#)
    outW = CLng((CDbl(tb.Width) * dpiX) / 72#)
    outH = CLng((CDbl(tb.Height) * dpiY) / 72#)
    If outW < 20 Or outH < 20 Then Exit Function
    MacroSplash_GetTxtExecutionLogScreenRectPixels = True
    Exit Function
Fail:
    MacroSplash_GetTxtExecutionLogScreenRectPixels = False
End Function

' cmd 繧偵Ο繧ｰ譫縺ｫ驥阪・繧九→縺阪∽ｺ碁㍾陦ｨ遉ｺ繧帝∩縺代ｋ縺溘ａ TextBox 繧剃ｸ譎る撼陦ｨ遉ｺ
Public Sub MacroSplash_BeginConsoleOverlay()
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    If m_splashConsoleOverlayActive Then Exit Sub
    MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog").Visible = False
    m_splashConsoleOverlayActive = True
    MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

Public Sub MacroSplash_EndConsoleOverlay()
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not m_splashConsoleOverlayActive Then Exit Sub
    m_splashConsoleOverlayActive = False
    If m_macroSplashShown Then
        MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog").Visible = True
        MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 繧ｳ繝ｳ繧ｽ繝ｼ繝ｫ譫縺ｮ邁｡譏馴勁蜴ｻ・・in32/Win64縲８T 繝帙せ繝・HWND 縺ｫ縺ｯ辟｡蜉ｹ縺ｪ蝣ｴ蜷医≠繧・窶・繧ｪ繝ｼ繝舌・繝ｬ繧､縺ｯ conhost 蠑ｷ蛻ｶ縺ｨ菴ｵ逕ｨ・・Public Sub MacroSplash_SetStep(ByVal stepMessage As String)
    Dim prevSU As Boolean
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    prevSU = Application.ScreenUpdating
    If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    MacroSplash_Form.lblMessage.caption = stepMessage
    MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
    DoEvents
    If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = False
End Sub

Public Sub MacroSplash_ClearExecutionLogPane()
    Dim tb As Object
    On Error Resume Next
    m_splashReadErrShown = False
    m_splashLastLogSnapshot = ""
    m_splashPollHaveCachedFileLen = False
    m_splashPollLastFileLen = 0
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    If Not SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    Set tb = MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog")
    If Not tb Is Nothing Then tb.text = ""
End Sub

' 繝ｭ繧ｰ縺ｯ譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺梧怙譁ｰ縲ゅく繝｣繝ｬ繝・ヨ繧呈怙蠕後↓鄂ｮ縺・txtExecutionLog 縺ｫ繝輔か繝ｼ繧ｫ繧ｹ・・serForm 縺ｫ縺ｯ SetFocus 縺後↑縺・ｼ・Public Sub MacroSplash_TextBoxScrollToTail(ByVal tb As Object)
    On Error Resume Next
    tb.HideSelection = False
    tb.SelStart = Len(tb.text)
    tb.SelLength = 0
    If Application.Interactive Then
        tb.SetFocus
    End If
    MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
    DoEvents
End Sub

' m_splashExecutionLogPath 縺ｮ UTF-8 繝ｭ繧ｰ繧・txtExecutionLog 縺ｸ・磯聞縺・→縺阪・譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺ｮ縺ｿ・・Public Sub MacroSplash_RefreshExecutionLogPane()
    Dim tb As Object
    Dim s As String
    Dim n As Long
    Dim prevSU As Boolean
    Dim errBanner As String
    Dim flen As Long
    Dim flenAtStart As Long
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    If Len(m_splashExecutionLogPath) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    Set tb = MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog")
    If tb Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    flenAtStart = -1
    If Len(Dir(m_splashExecutionLogPath)) > 0 Then
        flenAtStart = FileLen(m_splashExecutionLogPath)
        If Err.Number <> 0 Then Err.Clear: flenAtStart = -1
    End If
    If m_splashPollHaveCachedFileLen And flenAtStart >= 0 And flenAtStart = m_splashPollLastFileLen And Not m_splashReadErrShown Then
        Exit Sub
    End If
    s = GeminiReadUtf8File(m_splashExecutionLogPath)
    If Len(s) = 0 And Len(Dir(m_splashExecutionLogPath)) > 0 Then
        s = GeminiReadUtf8FileViaTempCopy(m_splashExecutionLogPath)
    End If
    n = Len(s)
    If n > 0 Then
        m_splashReadErrShown = False
        If n > SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS Then
            s = "窶ｦ・亥・鬆ｭ繧堤怐逡･縲ら峩霑代・縺ｿ陦ｨ遉ｺ・俄ｦ" & vbCrLf & Right$(s, SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS)
        End If
        If StrComp(s, m_splashLastLogSnapshot, vbBinaryCompare) = 0 Then
            m_splashPollLastFileLen = flenAtStart
            m_splashPollHaveCachedFileLen = True
            Exit Sub
        End If
        m_splashLastLogSnapshot = s
        m_splashPollLastFileLen = flenAtStart
        m_splashPollHaveCachedFileLen = True
        prevSU = Application.ScreenUpdating
        If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = True
        tb.text = s
        MacroSplash_TextBoxScrollToTail tb
        If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        Exit Sub
    End If
    If Len(Dir(m_splashExecutionLogPath)) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    flen = 0
    flen = FileLen(m_splashExecutionLogPath)
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then Err.Clear
    If flen = 0 And Len(tb.text) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    If m_splashReadErrShown Then Exit Sub
    m_splashPollHaveCachedFileLen = False
    errBanner = "縲舌Ο繧ｰ陦ｨ遉ｺ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縲粗xecution_log.txt 繧・VBA 縺九ｉ隱ｭ繧√∪縺帙ｓ縺ｧ縺励◆・・ython 縺後ヵ繧｡繧､繝ｫ繧帝幕縺・※縺・ｋ遲会ｼ峨・OG 繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医∪縺溘・繧ｨ繝・ぅ繧ｿ縺ｧ " & m_splashExecutionLogPath & " 繧堤峩謗･髢九＞縺ｦ遒ｺ隱阪＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・ & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
    prevSU = Application.ScreenUpdating
    If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    tb.text = errBanner & tb.text
    m_splashLastLogSnapshot = tb.text
    tb.SelStart = 1
    tb.SelLength = 0
    MacroSplash_Form.lblMessage.caption = "窶ｦ・亥ｮ溯｡後Ο繧ｰ縺ｮ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨・? 荳玖ｨ倥・縲舌Ο繧ｰ陦ｨ遉ｺ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縲代ｒ蜿ら・・・
    MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
    DoEvents
    If Not prevSU Then Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    m_splashReadErrShown = True
End Sub

' RunPython 邨ゆｺ・峩蠕後↑縺ｩ縲∝酔譛・Python 縺ｧ繝昴・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｰ縺ｧ縺阪↑縺九▲縺溘≠縺ｨ縺ｫ execution_log 繧剃ｸ諡ｬ陦ｨ遉ｺ・・nteractive 荳譎・True 縺ｧ謠冗判・・Public Sub MacroSplash_LoadExecutionLogFromPath(ByVal fullPath As String)
    Dim tb As Object
    Dim s As String
    Dim n As Long
    Dim prevInt As Boolean
    Dim errBanner As String
    Dim flen As Long
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    If Len(Dir(fullPath)) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    Set tb = MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog")
    If tb Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    s = GeminiReadUtf8File(fullPath)
    If Len(s) = 0 Then s = GeminiReadUtf8FileViaTempCopy(fullPath)
    n = Len(s)
    If n = 0 Then
        flen = FileLen(fullPath)
        If Err.Number <> 0 Then Err.Clear
        If flen > 0 Or Len(tb.text) > 0 Then
            errBanner = "縲舌Ο繧ｰ陦ｨ遉ｺ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ縲粗xecution_log.txt 繧定ｪｭ縺ｿ霎ｼ繧√∪縺帙ｓ縺ｧ縺励◆縲ゅヱ繧ｹ: " & fullPath & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
            prevInt = Application.Interactive
            Application.Interactive = True
            tb.text = errBanner & tb.text
            m_splashLastLogSnapshot = tb.text
            MacroSplash_Form.lblMessage.caption = "窶ｦ・亥ｮ溯｡後Ο繧ｰ縺ｮ荳諡ｬ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺ｫ螟ｱ謨・? 荳玖ｨ倥ｒ蜿ら・・・
            MacroSplash_Form.Repaint
            DoEvents
            If m_macroSplashLockedExcel Then Application.Interactive = False Else Application.Interactive = prevInt
        End If
        Exit Sub
    End If
    m_splashReadErrShown = False
    If n > SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS Then
        s = "窶ｦ・亥・鬆ｭ繧堤怐逡･縲ら峩霑代・縺ｿ陦ｨ遉ｺ・俄ｦ" & vbCrLf & Right$(s, SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS)
    End If
    prevInt = Application.Interactive
    Application.Interactive = True
    tb.text = s
    m_splashLastLogSnapshot = s
    MacroSplash_TextBoxScrollToTail tb
    If m_macroSplashLockedExcel Then
        Application.Interactive = False
    Else
        Application.Interactive = prevInt
    End If
End Sub

Public Sub MacroSplash_PositionDockExcelBottomCenter()
#If VBA7 Then
    Dim xlHwnd As LongPtr
    Dim splashHwnd As LongPtr
#Else
    Dim xlHwnd As Long
    Dim splashHwnd As Long
#End If
    Dim rcX As RECT
    Dim rcS As RECT
    Dim xlW As Long
    Dim sw As Long
    Dim sh As Long
    Dim newL As Long
    Dim newT As Long
    On Error GoTo SplashDockDone
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then GoTo SplashDockDone
#If VBA7 Then
    xlHwnd = Application.hwnd
#Else
    xlHwnd = Application.hwnd
#End If
    If xlHwnd = 0 Then GoTo SplashDockDone
    splashHwnd = FindWindow(0&, SPLASH_FORM_WINDOW_TITLE)
    If splashHwnd = 0 Then GoTo SplashDockDone
    If GetWindowRect(xlHwnd, rcX) = 0 Then GoTo SplashDockDone
    If GetWindowRect(splashHwnd, rcS) = 0 Then GoTo SplashDockDone
    xlW = rcX.Right - rcX.Left
    sw = rcS.Right - rcS.Left
    sh = rcS.Bottom - rcS.Top
    If xlW < 80 Or sw < 40 Or sh < 40 Then GoTo SplashDockDone
    newL = rcX.Left + (xlW - sw) \ 2
    newT = rcX.Bottom - sh - SPLASH_EXCEL_BOTTOM_GAP_PX
    Call SetWindowPos(splashHwnd, 0&, newL, newT, sw, sh, SWP_NOZORDER Or SWP_SHOWWINDOW)
SplashDockDone:
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 繝｢繝ｼ繝峨Ξ繧ｹ UserForm 縺瑚レ蠕後↓谿九ｋ縺ｨ蜀肴緒逕ｻ繝ｻ繝ｭ繧ｰ譖ｴ譁ｰ縺梧ｭ｢縺ｾ縺｣縺溘ｈ縺・↓隕九∴繧九％縺ｨ縺後≠繧九４how 逶ｴ蠕後↓蜑埼擇縺ｸ・医Θ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ縺後け繝ｪ繝・け縺励◆縺ｨ縺阪→蜷瑚ｶ｣譌ｨ・峨・Public Sub MacroSplash_BringFormToFront()
#If VBA7 Then
    Dim hwnd As LongPtr
#Else
    Dim hwnd As Long
#End If
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    MacroSplash_PositionDockExcelBottomCenter
    hwnd = FindWindow(0&, SPLASH_FORM_WINDOW_TITLE)
    If hwnd = 0 Then Exit Sub
    BringWindowToTop hwnd
    SetForegroundWindow hwnd
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

Public Sub MacroSplash_Show(Optional ByVal message As String, Optional ByVal lockExcelUI As Boolean = True)
    On Error GoTo CleanupFail
    If m_macroSplashShown Then MacroSplash_Hide
    m_animMacroSucceeded = False
    If Len(Trim$(message)) = 0 Then
        message = "蜃ｦ逅・ｸｭ縺ｧ縺吶ゅ＠縺ｰ繧峨￥縺雁ｾ・■縺上□縺輔＞縲・
    End If
    MacroSplash_Form.caption = SPLASH_FORM_WINDOW_TITLE
    MacroSplash_Form.lblMessage.caption = message
    MacroSplash_Form.StartUpPosition = 2  ' 蛻晄悄縺ｮ縺ｿ縲ら峩蠕後↓ MacroSplash_PositionDockExcelBottomCenter 縺ｧ Excel 荳狗ｫｯ荳ｭ螟ｮ縺ｸ
    m_macroSplashLockedExcel = False
    If lockExcelUI Then
        Application.Interactive = False
        m_macroSplashLockedExcel = True
    End If
    ' Show 縺ｮ Modal=False・医∪縺溘・逵∫払・峨〒繝｢繝ｼ繝峨Ξ繧ｹ縲ＷbModeless 縺ｯ蜿ら・險ｭ螳壹↓繧医▲縺ｦ譛ｪ螳夂ｾｩ縺ｫ縺ｪ繧九％縺ｨ縺後≠繧・    MacroSplash_Form.Show False
    m_macroSplashShown = True
    On Error Resume Next
    MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog").HideSelection = False
    MacroSplash_BringFormToFront
    DoEvents
    MacroStartBgm_StartIfAvailable
    Exit Sub
CleanupFail:
    On Error Resume Next
    If m_macroSplashLockedExcel Then Application.Interactive = True
    m_macroSplashLockedExcel = False
    m_macroSplashShown = False
    If Not m_frmMacroSplash Is Nothing Then
        Unload m_frmMacroSplash
    End If
    Set m_frmMacroSplash = Nothing
End Sub

Public Sub MacroSplash_Hide()
    On Error Resume Next
    MacroStartBgm_FadeOutAndClose
    m_splashConsoleOverlayActive = False
    If m_macroSplashShown Then
        If Not m_frmMacroSplash Is Nothing Then
            Unload m_frmMacroSplash
        End If
        Set m_frmMacroSplash = Nothing
    End If
    m_macroSplashShown = False
    If m_macroSplashLockedExcel Then
        Application.Interactive = True
        m_macroSplashLockedExcel = False
    End If
End Sub

' Python・・lwings・峨°繧牙他縺ｶ縲１M_AI_SPLASH_XLWINGS=1 譎ゅ・縺ｿ螳溯｡後＆繧後ｋ諠ｳ螳壹ゅ・繧ｯ繝ｭ蜷崎｡晉ｪ∵凾縺ｯ迺ｰ蠅・､画焚 PM_AI_XLWINGS_SPLASH_MACRO=讓呎ｺ悶Δ繧ｸ繝･繝ｼ繝ｫ蜷・SplashLog_AppendChunk
Public Sub SplashLog_AppendChunk(ByVal chunk As String)
    On Error Resume Next
    If Len(chunk) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    If Not SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() Then Exit Sub
    If Not m_macroSplashShown Then Exit Sub
    Dim tb As Object
    Set tb = MacroSplash_Form.Controls("txtExecutionLog")
    If tb Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    Dim n As Long
    n = Len(tb.text) + Len(chunk)
    If n > SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS Then
        tb.text = Right$(tb.text & chunk, SPLASH_LOG_MAX_DISPLAY_CHARS)
    Else
        tb.text = tb.text & chunk
    End If
    MacroSplash_TextBoxScrollToTail tb
End Sub

' 繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″_* 縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺暦ｼ壹せ繝励Λ繝・す繝･陦ｨ遉ｺ 竊・繝槭け繝ｭ螳溯｡鯉ｼ亥ｼ墓焚縺ｯ譛螟ｧ2縺､縺ｾ縺ｧ Application.Run 縺ｫ蟋碑ｭｲ・・' lockExcelUI・哥alse = InputBox・上ヵ繧ｩ繝ｳ繝医ム繧､繧｢繝ｭ繧ｰ縺ｪ縺ｩ Excel 蟇ｾ隧ｱ縺悟ｿ・ｦ√↑繝槭け繝ｭ蜷代￠
' allowMacroSound・啜rue = 谿ｵ髫・・乗ｮｵ髫・縺ｨ蜷梧ｧ倥↓ BGM繝ｻ謌仙粥譎ゅメ繝｣繧､繝繧定ｨｱ蜿ｯ・域里螳・False・・Public Sub 繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″_繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･莉倥″縺ｧ螳溯｡・ByVal splashMessage As String, ByVal procName As String, Optional ByVal arg1 As Variant, Optional ByVal arg2 As Variant, Optional ByVal lockExcelUI As Boolean = True, Optional ByVal allowMacroSound As Boolean = False)
    m_splashAllowMacroSound = allowMacroSound
    On Error GoTo EH
    MacroSplash_Show splashMessage, lockExcelUI
    If IsMissing(arg1) And IsMissing(arg2) Then
        Application.Run procName
    ElseIf Not IsMissing(arg1) And IsMissing(arg2) Then
        Application.Run procName, arg1
    Else
        Application.Run procName, arg1, arg2
    End If
    GoTo Finish
EH:
    On Error Resume Next
Finish:
    MacroStartBgm_FadeOutAndClose
    If m_animMacroSucceeded Then
        On Error Resume Next
        MacroCompleteChime
    End If
    MacroSplash_Hide
    m_splashAllowMacroSound = False
End Sub

VBA MACRO 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ謗｢邏｢.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ謗｢邏｢'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit

Function GetLatestOutputFile(folderPath As String, filePattern As String) As String
    Dim latestPath As String
    Dim latestDate As Date

    If Len(Dir(folderPath, vbDirectory)) = 0 Then
        GetLatestOutputFile = ""
        Exit Function
    End If

    latestDate = 0
    latestPath = ""
    CollectLatestOutputFileRecursive folderPath, filePattern, latestPath, latestDate
    GetLatestOutputFile = latestPath
End Function

Public Sub CollectLatestOutputFileRecursive(ByVal folderPath As String, ByVal filePattern As String, ByRef latestPath As String, ByRef latestDate As Date)
    Dim fso As Object
    Dim fldr As Object
    Dim subFldr As Object
    Dim fil As Object
    Dim currDate As Date
    If Len(folderPath) = 0 Then Exit Sub

    On Error Resume Next
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    If fso Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    If Not fso.FolderExists(folderPath) Then Exit Sub
    Set fldr = fso.GetFolder(folderPath)
    If fldr Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    On Error GoTo 0

    For Each fil In fldr.Files
        If LCase$(fil.Name) Like LCase$(filePattern) Then
            On Error Resume Next
            currDate = fil.DateLastModified
            If Err.Number = 0 Then
                If currDate > latestDate Then
                    latestDate = currDate
                    latestPath = CStr(fil.path)
                End If
            Else
                Err.Clear
            End If
            On Error GoTo 0
        End If
    Next fil

    For Each subFldr In fldr.SubFolders
        CollectLatestOutputFileRecursive CStr(subFldr.path), filePattern, latestPath, latestDate
    Next subFldr
End Sub

' =========================================================
' 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ謗｢邏｢・域怙譁ｰ縺ｮ蜃ｺ蜉帙ヵ繧｡繧､繝ｫ繝代せ繧定ｿ斐☆・・' GetLatestOutputFile:
'   folderPath 驟堺ｸ九ｒ蜀榊ｸｰ逧・↓襍ｰ譟ｻ縺励’ilePattern・・ike 繝代ち繝ｼ繝ｳ・峨↓荳閾ｴ縺吶ｋ繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ縺ｮ縺・■
'   DateLastModified 縺梧怙螟ｧ縺ｮ繧ゅ・縺ｮ繝輔Ν繝代せ繧定ｿ斐☆縲りｩｲ蠖薙↑縺励・繝輔か繝ｫ繝荳肴ｭ｣譎ゅ・ "" 縲・' CollectLatestOutputFileRecursive:
'   荳願ｨ倥・蜀・Κ蜃ｦ逅・４cripting.FileSystemObject 縺ｧ Files / SubFolders 繧定ｾｿ繧九・' =========================================================

VBA MACRO 繝輔か繝ｳ繝育ｮ｡逅・bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/繝輔か繝ｳ繝育ｮ｡逅・

Option Explicit

Public Function GetOrCreateFontScratchSheet() As Worksheet
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SCRATCH_SHEET_FONT)
    On Error GoTo 0
    If ws Is Nothing Then
        Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets.Add(After:=ThisWorkbook.Sheets(ThisWorkbook.Sheets.Count))
        On Error Resume Next
        ws.Name = SCRATCH_SHEET_FONT
        On Error GoTo 0
        ws.Range("A1").Value = "・医ヵ繧ｩ繝ｳ繝磯∈謚樒畑繝ｻ蜑企勁縺励↑縺・〒縺上□縺輔＞・・
        ws.Visible = xlSheetVeryHidden
    End If
    Set GetOrCreateFontScratchSheet = ws
End Function

Public Sub RestoreCellFontProps(ByVal r As Range, ByVal oldName As String, _
    ByVal oldSize As Variant, ByVal oldBold As Variant, ByVal oldItalic As Variant, _
    ByVal oldUnderline As Variant, ByVal oldColor As Variant, ByVal oldStrike As Variant)
    On Error Resume Next
    With r.Font
        .Name = oldName
        If Not IsEmpty(oldSize) Then .Size = oldSize
        If Not IsEmpty(oldBold) Then .Bold = oldBold
        If Not IsEmpty(oldItalic) Then .Italic = oldItalic
        If Not IsEmpty(oldUnderline) Then .Underline = oldUnderline
        If Not IsEmpty(oldColor) Then .Color = oldColor
        If Not IsEmpty(oldStrike) Then .Strikethrough = oldStrike
    End With
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

Public Function FontNameExistsInExcel(ByVal fontName As String) As Boolean
    Dim i As Long
    For i = 1 To Application.FontNames.Count
        If StrComp(Application.FontNames(i), fontName, vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
            FontNameExistsInExcel = True
            Exit Function
        End If
    Next i
End Function

Public Sub ApplyFontToAllSheetCells(ByVal fontName As String, ByRef skippedOut As String)
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim ur As Range
    Dim rangeErr As Boolean
    
    skippedOut = ""
    For Each ws In ThisWorkbook.Worksheets
        On Error Resume Next
        rangeErr = False
        Set ur = Nothing
        Set ur = ws.UsedRange
        If Err.Number <> 0 Then
            skippedOut = skippedOut & "繝ｻ" & ws.Name & "・・sedRange: " & Err.Description & "・・ & vbCrLf
            Err.Clear
            rangeErr = True
        End If
        If Not rangeErr Then
            ur.Font.Name = fontName
            If Err.Number <> 0 Then
                skippedOut = skippedOut & "繝ｻ" & ws.Name & "・・ont.Name: " & Err.Description & "・・ & vbCrLf
                Err.Clear
            End If
        End If
        On Error GoTo 0
    Next ws
End Sub

    Dim skipped As String
    On Error Resume Next
    ApplyFontToAllSheetCells BIZ_UDP_GOTHIC_FONT_NAME, skipped

    驟榊床繝槭け繝ｭ_蟇ｾ雎｡繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医ｒ譚｡莉ｶ縺ｩ縺翫ｊ縺ｫ菫晁ｭｷ
    On Error GoTo 0
    MsgBox "繝輔か繝ｳ繝郁ｨｭ螳壹〒繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: " & Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub

'==============================================================================
' 蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ ? 陦ｨ遉ｺ蛻・B)縺ｨ騾｣蜍輔☆繧九ヵ繧ｩ繝ｼ繝縺ｮ繝√ぉ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ繧帝・鄂ｮ
' 髢狗匱繧ｿ繝・竊・謖ｿ蜈･ 竊・繝輔か繝ｼ繝 繧ｳ繝ｳ繝医Ο繝ｼ繝ｫ縺ｮ縲後メ繧ｧ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ縲阪→蜷檎ｭ峨・' 蜀榊ｮ溯｡後☆繧九→譌｢蟄倥・繝√ぉ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ繧貞炎髯､縺励※莉倥￠逶ｴ縺励∪縺呻ｼ医そ繝ｫ縺ｮ TRUE/FALSE 縺ｯ菫晄戟・峨・'==============================================================================
Public Sub 蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_繝√ぉ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ繧帝・鄂ｮ()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim r As Long
    Dim lastR As Long
    Dim cb As CheckBox
    Dim rng As Range
    Dim linkAddr As String

    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_COL_CONFIG_RESULT_TASK)
    On Error GoTo 0
    If ws Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医・ & SHEET_COL_CONFIG_RESULT_TASK & "縲阪′隕九▽縺九ｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・, vbExclamation, "蛻苓ｨｭ螳・
        Exit Sub
    End If

    On Error GoTo FailChk
    Do While ws.CheckBoxes.Count > 0
        ws.CheckBoxes(1).Delete
    Loop

    lastR = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.Count, 1).End(xlUp).Row
    If lastR < 2 Then
        MsgBox "繝・・繧ｿ陦後′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ・・陦檎岼縺ｯ隕句・縺励・陦檎岼莉･髯阪↓蛻怜錐繧貞・繧後※縺上□縺輔＞・峨・, vbInformation
        Exit Sub
    End If

    linkAddr = "'" & Replace(ws.Name, "'", "''") & "'!"

    For r = 2 To lastR
        If Len(Trim$(CStr(ws.Cells(r, 1).Value))) = 0 Then GoTo NextLoop

        Set rng = ws.Cells(r, 2)
        If Len(Trim$(CStr(rng.Value))) = 0 Then
            rng.Value = True
        End If

        Set cb = ws.CheckBoxes.Add(rng.Left + 2, rng.Top + 0.5, 50, 14)
        With cb
            .LinkedCell = linkAddr & rng.Address(True, True)
            .caption = ""
        End With
NextLoop:
    Next r

    MsgBox "繝√ぉ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ繧帝・鄂ｮ縺励∪縺励◆縲・ & vbCrLf & _
        "陦ｨ遉ｺ蛻・B)縺ｮ TRUE/FALSE 縺ｨ騾｣蜍輔＠縺ｾ縺吶・, vbInformation
    Exit Sub

FailChk:
    MsgBox "繝√ぉ繝・け繝懊ャ繧ｯ繧ｹ驟咲ｽｮ縺ｧ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: " & Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub

' 蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ 竊・邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ 縺ｸ蛻鈴・・蛻鈴撼陦ｨ遉ｺ繧帝←逕ｨ・・ython / xlwings・・' 蝗ｳ蠖｢縺ｮ繝槭け繝ｭ: 縲後い繝九Γ莉倥″_蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_蛻鈴・｡ｨ遉ｺ繧単ython驕ｩ逕ｨ縲搾ｼ域款荳九い繝九Γ莉倥″・峨・'   驥崎､・・蜷阪・謨ｴ逅・・縺ｿ: 縲後い繝九Γ莉倥″_蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_驥崎､・・蜷阪ｒ謨ｴ逅・阪・'   譛ｬ菴薙ｒ逶ｴ謖・ｮ壹☆繧九→ AnimateButtonPush 縺悟虚縺九↑縺・・' 繝ｻ莠句燕縺ｫ縲悟・險ｭ螳壹阪す繝ｼ繝医〒蛻怜錐繝ｻ陦ｨ遉ｺ繧堤ｷｨ髮・＠縺ｦ縺九ｉ螳溯｡後・' 繝ｻExcel 縺ｧ譛ｬ繝悶ャ繧ｯ繧帝幕縺・◆縺ｾ縺ｾ・・lwings 縺梧磁邯夲ｼ峨ゆｿ晏ｭ倥＠縺ｦ縺九ｉ螳溯｡梧耳螂ｨ縲・'==============================================================================
Public Sub 蛻苓ｨｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_蛻鈴・｡ｨ遉ｺ繧単ython驕ｩ逕ｨ()
    Dim wsh As Object
    Dim runBat As String
    Dim targetDir As String
    Dim exitCode As Long
    Dim wsRes As Worksheet
    Dim wsCfg As Worksheet
    Dim prevScreen As Boolean

    targetDir = ThisWorkbook.path
    If Len(targetDir) = 0 Then
        MsgBox "蜈医↓縺薙・ Excel 繝輔ぃ繧､繝ｫ繧剃ｿ晏ｭ倥＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・, vbExclamation, "蛻苓ｨｭ螳壹・驕ｩ逕ｨ"
        Exit Sub
    End If

    On Error Resume Next
    Set wsRes = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_RESULT_TASK_LIST)
    Set wsCfg = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_COL_CONFIG_RESULT_TASK)
    On Error GoTo 0
    If wsRes Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医・ & SHEET_RESULT_TASK_LIST & "縲阪′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・, vbExclamation, "蛻苓ｨｭ螳壹・驕ｩ逕ｨ"
        Exit Sub
    End If
    If wsCfg Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医・ & SHEET_COL_CONFIG_RESULT_TASK & "縲阪′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・, vbExclamation, "蛻苓ｨｭ螳壹・驕ｩ逕ｨ"
        Exit Sub
    End If

    On Error Resume Next
    ThisWorkbook.Save
    On Error GoTo 0

    Set wsh = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
    wsh.Environment("Process")("TASK_INPUT_WORKBOOK") = ThisWorkbook.FullName

    prevScreen = Application.ScreenUpdating
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    MacroSplash_SetStep "蛻苓ｨｭ螳・ Python 縺ｧ邨先棡繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ縺ｮ蛻鈴・・陦ｨ遉ｺ繧帝←逕ｨ縺励※縺・∪縺吮ｦ"
    runBat = "@echo off" & vbCrLf & "pushd """ & targetDir & """" & vbCrLf & "chcp 65001>nul" & vbCrLf & _
             "py -3 -u python\apply_result_task_column_layout.py" & vbCrLf & _
             "echo." & vbCrLf & _
             "echo [column-layout] ERRORLEVEL=%ERRORLEVEL%" & vbCrLf & _
             "exit /b %ERRORLEVEL%"
    exitCode = RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout(wsh, runBat)
    Application.ScreenUpdating = prevScreen

    On Error Resume Next
    Set wsRes = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_RESULT_TASK_LIST)
    If Not wsRes Is Nothing Then
        邨先棡繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・蛻怜ｹ・AutoFit髱櫁｡ｨ遉ｺ繧堤ｶｭ謖・wsRes
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0

    If exitCode <> 0 Then
        MsgBox "Python 縺ｮ邨ゆｺ・さ繝ｼ繝峨′ " & CStr(exitCode) & " 縺ｧ縺吶・ & vbCrLf _
            & "log\execution_log.txt 繧堤｢ｺ隱阪＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・, vbExclamation, "蛻苓ｨｭ螳壹・驕ｩ逕ｨ"
    Else
        MacroSplash_SetStep "縲・ & SHEET_RESULT_TASK_LIST & "縲阪・蛻鈴・・陦ｨ遉ｺ繧偵・ & SHEET_COL_CONFIG_RESULT_TASK & "縲阪↓蜷医ｏ縺帙∪縺励◆縲・
        m_animMacroSucceeded = True
    End If
End Sub

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    MacroSplash_SetStep "驟榊床險育判: 驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・分繧貞ｰ乗焚繧ｭ繝ｼ縺ｧ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺医※縺・∪縺吮ｦ"
    runBat = "@echo off" & vbCrLf & "pushd """ & targetDir & """" & vbCrLf & "chcp 65001>nul" & vbCrLf & _
             "py -3 -u python\apply_plan_input_dispatch_trial_order_sort_by_float_keys.py" & vbCrLf & _
             "echo." & vbCrLf & _
             "echo [plan-dispatch-trial-float-keys] ERRORLEVEL=%ERRORLEVEL%" & vbCrLf & _
             "exit /b %ERRORLEVEL%"
    exitCode = RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout(wsh, runBat)
    Application.ScreenUpdating = prevScreen

    If exitCode <> 0 Then
        MsgBox "Python 縺ｮ邨ゆｺ・さ繝ｼ繝峨′ " & CStr(exitCode) & " 縺ｧ縺吶・ & vbCrLf _
            & "log\execution_log.txt 繧堤｢ｺ隱阪＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・, vbExclamation, "隧ｦ陦碁・・荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺・
    Else
        MacroSplash_SetStep "縲・ & SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK & "縲阪・驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・分繧偵く繝ｼ鬆・↓荳ｦ縺ｹ縲・ 縺九ｉ謖ｯ繧顔峩縺励∪縺励◆縲・
        m_animMacroSucceeded = True
    End If
End Sub

' 繧ｰ繝ｩ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・句ｽｱ莉倥″蝗ｳ蠖｢・医Γ繧､繝ｳ縺ｮ縲後°縺｣縺薙＞縺・・繧ｿ繝ｳ縲阪→蜷瑚ｶ｣譌ｨ・峨ＴhapeName 縺ｧ蝗ｳ蠖｢蜷阪ｒ蛹ｺ蛻･縺吶ｋ縲・Private Sub PlanInputSheet_AddGradientActionButton( _
    ByVal ws As Worksheet, _
    ByVal btnText As String, _
    ByVal onActionFull As String, _
    ByVal leftPt As Single, _
    ByVal topPt As Single, _
    ByVal colorTop As Long, _
    ByVal colorBottom As Long, _
    ByVal shapeName As String)
    Dim shp As Shape
    Const BTN_W As Single = 268
    Const BTN_H As Single = 48
    Set shp = ws.Shapes.AddShape(msoShapeRoundedRectangle, leftPt, topPt, BTN_W, BTN_H)
    shp.Name = shapeName
    With shp
        With .TextFrame2.TextRange
            .text = btnText
            .Font.Name = "繝｡繧､繝ｪ繧ｪ"
            .Font.Size = 12
            .Font.Bold = msoTrue
            .Font.Fill.ForeColor.RGB = RGB(255, 255, 255)
        End With
        .TextFrame2.VerticalAnchor = msoAnchorMiddle
        .TextFrame2.TextRange.ParagraphFormat.Alignment = msoAlignCenter
        With .Fill
            .Visible = msoTrue
            .TwoColorGradient Style:=msoGradientVertical, Variant:=1
            .ForeColor.RGB = colorTop
            .BackColor.RGB = colorBottom
        End With
        .line.Visible = msoFalse
        With .ThreeD
            .BevelTopType = msoBevelSoftRound
            .BevelTopDepth = 6
            .BevelTopInset = 6
        End With
        With .Shadow
            .Type = msoShadow21
            .Visible = msoTrue
            .OffsetX = 3
            .OffsetY = 3
            .Transparency = 0.5
            .Blur = 4
        End With
        .OnAction = onActionFull
    End With
End Sub

'==============================================================================
' 驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉・ 荳願ｨ倥碁・蜿ｰ隧ｦ陦碁・ｒ蜀崎ｨ育ｮ励咲畑縺ｮ繧ｰ繝ｩ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ蝗ｳ蠖｢繧・1 陦檎岼莉倩ｿ代↓驟咲ｽｮ
' 髢狗匱繧ｿ繝・竊・繝槭け繝ｭ 竊・縲碁・蜿ｰ險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・險育ｮ励・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ縲阪∪縺溘・
' 縲後い繝九Γ莉倥″_驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・險育ｮ励・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ縲・'==============================================================================
Public Sub 驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・險育ｮ励・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim ur As Range
    Dim anchorCol As Long
    Dim leftPt As Single
    Dim topPt As Single
    Dim sh As Shape
    Dim wbQuoted As String
    Dim macroAnim As String
    Dim i As Long
    On Error GoTo FailBtn
    Set ws = Nothing
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK)
    On Error GoTo FailBtn
    If ws Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医・ & SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK & "縲阪′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・, vbExclamation, "驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・繧ｿ繝ｳ"
        Exit Sub
    End If
    On Error Resume Next
    For i = ws.Shapes.Count To 1 Step -1
        Set sh = ws.Shapes(i)
        If StrComp(sh.Name, SHAPE_PLAN_INPUT_DISPATCH_TRIAL_ORDER, vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
            sh.Delete
        End If
    Next i
    On Error GoTo FailBtn
    Set ur = Nothing
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ur = ws.UsedRange
    On Error GoTo FailBtn
    anchorCol = 4
    If Not ur Is Nothing Then
        anchorCol = ur.Column + ur.Columns.Count + 1
        If anchorCol < 4 Then anchorCol = 4
        If anchorCol > 80 Then anchorCol = 80
    End If
    leftPt = ws.Cells(1, anchorCol).Left
    topPt = ws.Rows(1).Top + 1.5
    wbQuoted = "'" & Replace(ThisWorkbook.Name, "'", "''") & "'"
    macroAnim = wbQuoted & "!繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″_驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・分繧貞・險育ｮ・
    PlanInputSheet_AddGradientActionButton ws, "驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・ｒ譖ｴ譁ｰ", macroAnim, leftPt, topPt, RGB(100, 120, 220), RGB(40, 50, 120), SHAPE_PLAN_INPUT_DISPATCH_TRIAL_ORDER
    ws.Activate
    On Error Resume Next
    ws.Range("A1").Select
    On Error GoTo 0
    MsgBox "縲・ & SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK & "縲阪↓繝懊ち繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ縺励∪縺励◆縲・ & vbCrLf & _
           "・磯・蜿ｰ荳崎ｦ√ｒ謇句虚縺ｧ繧ｯ繝ｪ繧｢縺励◆縺ゅ→縲√け繝ｪ繝・け縺ｧ隧ｦ陦碁・ｒ蜀崎ｨ育ｮ励＠縺ｾ縺呻ｼ・, vbInformation, "驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・繧ｿ繝ｳ"
    Exit Sub
FailBtn:
    MsgBox "繝懊ち繝ｳ驟咲ｽｮ縺ｧ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: " & Err.Description, vbCritical, "驟榊床隧ｦ陦碁・・繧ｿ繝ｳ"
End Sub

'==============================================================================
' 驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉・ 縲悟ｰ乗焚繧ｭ繝ｼ縺ｧ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺遺・1..n縲咲畑繧ｰ繝ｩ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ蝗ｳ蠖｢繧・1 陦檎岼莉倩ｿ代↓驟咲ｽｮ・亥・險育ｮ励・繧ｿ繝ｳ縺ｮ荳具ｼ・' 髢狗匱繧ｿ繝・竊・繝槭け繝ｭ 竊・縲碁・蜿ｰ險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽隧ｦ陦碁・ｰ乗焚繧ｭ繝ｼ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺医・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ縲・'==============================================================================
Public Sub 驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽隧ｦ陦碁・ｰ乗焚繧ｭ繝ｼ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺医・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim ur As Range
    Dim anchorCol As Long
    Dim leftPt As Single
    Dim topPt As Single
    Dim sh As Shape
    Dim wbQuoted As String
    Dim macroAnim As String
    Dim i As Long
    Const BTN_H As Single = 48
    Const BTN_GAP As Single = 6
    On Error GoTo FailBtn2
    Set ws = Nothing
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK)
    On Error GoTo FailBtn2
    If ws Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医・ & SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK & "縲阪′縺ゅｊ縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲・, vbExclamation, "隧ｦ陦碁・く繝ｼ繝懊ち繝ｳ"
        Exit Sub
    End If
    On Error Resume Next
    For i = ws.Shapes.Count To 1 Step -1
        Set sh = ws.Shapes(i)
        If StrComp(sh.Name, SHAPE_PLAN_INPUT_DISPATCH_TRIAL_ORDER_FLOAT_KEYS, vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
            sh.Delete
        End If
    Next i
    On Error GoTo FailBtn2
    Set ur = Nothing
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ur = ws.UsedRange
    On Error GoTo FailBtn2
    anchorCol = 4
    If Not ur Is Nothing Then
        anchorCol = ur.Column + ur.Columns.Count + 1
        If anchorCol < 4 Then anchorCol = 4
        If anchorCol > 80 Then anchorCol = 80
    End If
    leftPt = ws.Cells(1, anchorCol).Left
    topPt = ws.Rows(1).Top + 1.5 + BTN_H + BTN_GAP
    wbQuoted = "'" & Replace(ThisWorkbook.Name, "'", "''") & "'"
    macroAnim = wbQuoted & "!繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″_驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉媽隧ｦ陦碁・ｒ蟆乗焚繧ｭ繝ｼ縺ｧ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺・
    PlanInputSheet_AddGradientActionButton ws, "隧ｦ陦碁・ｒ繧ｭ繝ｼ縺ｧ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺・, macroAnim, leftPt, topPt, RGB(0, 150, 140), RGB(0, 75, 70), SHAPE_PLAN_INPUT_DISPATCH_TRIAL_ORDER_FLOAT_KEYS
    ws.Activate
    On Error Resume Next
    ws.Range("A1").Select
    On Error GoTo 0
    MsgBox "縲・ & SHEET_PLAN_INPUT_TASK & "縲阪↓繝懊ち繝ｳ繧帝・鄂ｮ縺励∪縺励◆縲・ & vbCrLf & _
           "・磯・蜿ｰ隧ｦ陦碁・分縺ｫ 1, 2, 1.5 縺ｪ縺ｩ繧ｭ繝ｼ繧貞・繧後◆縺ゅ→縲√け繝ｪ繝・け縺ｧ譏・・↓荳ｦ縺ｹ 1 縺九ｉ謖ｯ繧顔峩縺励∪縺呻ｼ・, vbInformation, "隧ｦ陦碁・く繝ｼ繝懊ち繝ｳ"
    Exit Sub
FailBtn2:
    MsgBox "繝懊ち繝ｳ驟咲ｽｮ縺ｧ繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ: " & Err.Description, vbCritical, "隧ｦ陦碁・く繝ｼ繝懊ち繝ｳ"
End Sub

' 谿ｵ髫・/2 cmd 髱櫁｡ｨ遉ｺ: 繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医瑚ｨｭ螳喟迺ｰ蠅・､画焚縲喉 蛻・STAGE12_CMD_HIDE_WINDOW 縺九▽ B 髱樒ｩｺ 竊・縺昴・蛟､縲よ悴險ｭ螳壹↑繧・Environ("STAGE12_CMD_HIDE_WINDOW")縲ゅ←縺｡繧峨ｂ遨ｺ縺ｪ繧・STAGE12_CMD_HIDE_WINDOW 螳壽焚縲・


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
VBA MACRO 讌ｭ蜍吶Ο繧ｸ繝・け.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/讌ｭ蜍吶Ο繧ｸ繝・け'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit

Public Function EnsureStageBatchStdoutRedirect(ByVal body As String) As String
    Dim t As String
    Dim lines() As String
    Dim i As Long
    Dim s As String
    t = Replace(Replace(body, vbCrLf, vbLf), vbCr, vbLf)
    lines = Split(t, vbLf)
    For i = LBound(lines) To UBound(lines)
        s = lines(i)
        If Len(s) > 0 Then
            If InStr(1, LTrim$(s), "py ", vbTextCompare) = 1 Then
                If InStr(1, s, "1>>", vbTextCompare) = 0 And InStr(1, s, ">nul", vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
                    lines(i) = RTrim$(s) & " 1>nul 2>&1"
                End If
                EnsureStageBatchStdoutRedirect = Join(lines, vbCrLf)
                Exit Function
            End If
        End If
    Next i
    EnsureStageBatchStdoutRedirect = body
End Function

Public Function RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout(ByVal wsh As Object, ByVal body As String, Optional ByVal applyTopQuarterFullWidthConsole As Boolean = False, Optional ByVal hideCmdWindow As Boolean = False) As Long
    Dim p As String
    Dim uniq As String
    Dim batText As String
    ' D3=false: STAGE12_D3FALSE_SPLASH_CONSOLE_LAYOUT 縺九▽繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･譎ゅ・縺ｿ繧ｪ繝ｼ繝舌・繝ｬ繧､逕ｨ Exec縲ゅ◎繧御ｻ･螟悶・蜷梧悄 Run・医え繧｣繝ｳ繝峨え繝ｬ繧､繧｢繧ｦ繝医・ OS 莉ｻ縺幢ｼ・    If Not SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() Then
        ' 繝ｭ繧ｰ譫繧ｪ繝ｼ繝舌・繝ｬ繧､縺ｯ縲瑚ｦ九∴繧九さ繝ｳ繧ｽ繝ｼ繝ｫ縲榊燕謠舌る撼陦ｨ遉ｺ謖・ｮ壽凾縺ｯ D3=true 邨瑚ｷｯ縺ｨ蜷梧ｧ倥↓ headless 縺ｸ縲・        If m_macroSplashShown And STAGE12_D3FALSE_SPLASH_CONSOLE_LAYOUT And Not hideCmdWindow Then
            Randomize
            uniq = "PM_AI_CMD_" & Format(Now, "yyyymmddhhnnss") & "_" & CStr(Int(1000000 * Rnd))
            batText = AugmentCmdBodyWithConsoleTitle(body, uniq)
            p = WriteTempCmdFile(batText)
            RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout = RunCmdFileStageExecAndPoll(wsh, p, uniq, False, False, True)
        ElseIf hideCmdWindow Or applyTopQuarterFullWidthConsole Then
            batText = body
            If hideCmdWindow Then batText = EnsureStageBatchStdoutRedirect(batText)
            Randomize
            uniq = "PM_AI_" & Format(Now, "yyyymmddhhnnss") & "_" & CStr(Int(1000000 * Rnd))
            batText = AugmentCmdBodyWithConsoleTitle(batText, uniq)
            p = WriteTempCmdFile(batText)
            RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout = RunCmdFileStageExecAndPoll(wsh, p, uniq, applyTopQuarterFullWidthConsole And Not hideCmdWindow, hideCmdWindow, False)
        Else
            p = WriteTempCmdFile(body)
            RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout = RunCmdFileStageExecAndPoll(wsh, p, "", False, False, False)
        End If
        GoTo RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayoutCleanup
    End If
    If hideCmdWindow Or applyTopQuarterFullWidthConsole Then
        batText = body
        If hideCmdWindow Then batText = EnsureStageBatchStdoutRedirect(batText)
        Randomize
        uniq = "PM_AI_" & Format(Now, "yyyymmddhhnnss") & "_" & CStr(Int(1000000 * Rnd))
        batText = AugmentCmdBodyWithConsoleTitle(batText, uniq)
        p = WriteTempCmdFile(batText)
        RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout = RunCmdFileStageExecAndPoll(wsh, p, uniq, applyTopQuarterFullWidthConsole And Not hideCmdWindow, hideCmdWindow)
    Else
        p = WriteTempCmdFile(body)
        RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayout = RunCmdFileWithConsoleLayout(wsh, p)
    End If
RunTempCmdWithConsoleLayoutCleanup:
    On Error Resume Next
    Kill p
    On Error GoTo 0
End Function

Public Function GetMainWorksheet() As Worksheet
    ' 驟榊床繝悶ャ繧ｯ縺ｮ繝｡繧､繝ｳ UI 縺ｯ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝亥錐縲後Γ繧､繝ｳ_縲榊崋螳夲ｼ域立縲後Γ繧､繝ｳ縲阪勲ain縲阪ｄ驛ｨ蛻・ｸ閾ｴ縺ｯ菴ｿ繧上↑縺・ｼ・    On Error Resume Next
    Set GetMainWorksheet = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets("繝｡繧､繝ｳ_")
    On Error GoTo 0
End Function

' planning_core 縺・log\gemini_usage_summary_for_main.txt・・TF-8・峨↓蜃ｺ蜉帙＠縺・Gemini 蛻ｩ逕ｨ繧ｵ繝槭Μ繧偵・' 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・P16 莉･髯阪↓蜿肴丐縺吶ｋ縲Ｐpenpyxl 縺御ｿ晏ｭ倥〒縺阪↑縺・ｼ医ヶ繝・け髢九″縺｣縺ｱ縺ｪ縺暦ｼ峨→縺咲畑縲よｮｵ髫・/2 繧ｳ繧｢縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｶ縲・Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・Gemini蛻ｩ逕ｨ繧ｵ繝槭Μ繧単蛻励↓蜿肴丐(ByVal targetDir As String)
    Const START_ROW As Long = 16
    Const USAGE_COL As Long = 16 ' P
    Const CLEAR_ROWS As Long = 120
    
    Dim wsMain As Worksheet
    Dim fp As String
    Dim adoStream As Object
    Dim outputText As String
    Dim logLines() As String
    Dim i As Long
    Dim r As Long
    Dim lastClearRow As Long
    
    Set wsMain = GetMainWorksheet()
    If wsMain Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    
    lastClearRow = START_ROW + CLEAR_ROWS - 1
    wsMain.Range(wsMain.Cells(START_ROW, USAGE_COL), wsMain.Cells(lastClearRow, USAGE_COL)).ClearContents
    
    fp = targetDir & "\log\gemini_usage_summary_for_main.txt"
    If Len(Dir(fp)) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    On Error GoTo GeminiUsageP_Fail
    Set adoStream = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
    adoStream.charset = "UTF-8"
    adoStream.Open
    adoStream.LoadFromFile fp
    outputText = adoStream.ReadText
    adoStream.Close
    Set adoStream = Nothing
    On Error GoTo 0
    
    outputText = Replace(outputText, vbCrLf, vbLf)
    If Len(Trim$(outputText)) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    logLines = Split(outputText, vbLf)
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    For i = LBound(logLines) To UBound(logLines)
        r = START_ROW + i
        If r > lastClearRow Then Exit For
        With wsMain.Cells(r, USAGE_COL)
            .Value = logLines(i)
            .WrapText = True
            .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
        End With
    Next i
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    Exit Sub
    
GeminiUsageP_Fail:
    On Error Resume Next
    If Not adoStream Is Nothing Then
        adoStream.Close
        Set adoStream = Nothing
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医ｒ陦ｨ遉ｺ縺・A1 繧偵い繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝悶↓縺吶ｋ・医す繝ｼ繝亥錐縲後Γ繧､繝ｳ_縲搾ｼ扁etMainWorksheet 縺ｨ蜷後§・・Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・1繧帝∈謚・)
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = GetMainWorksheet()
    If ws Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    ws.Activate
    ws.Range("A1").Select
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' Ctrl+Shift+繝・Φ繧ｭ繝ｼ - 逕ｨ・域焔邯壹″蜷阪・蠕捺擂莠呈鋤縺ｧ CtrlShift0 縺ｮ縺ｾ縺ｾ縲・pplication.OnKey 縺ｮ Procedure 縺ｯ ASCII 蜷阪′辟｡髮｣・・Public Function FindColHeader(ws As Worksheet, ByVal headerText As String) As Long
    Dim c As Long
    Dim lastCol As Long
    lastCol = ws.Cells(1, ws.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    For c = 1 To lastCol
        If Trim$(CStr(ws.Cells(1, c).Value)) = headerText Then
            FindColHeader = c
            Exit Function
        End If
    Next c
    FindColHeader = 0
End Function

' 繝上う繝代・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ蜀堺ｻ倅ｸ主ｾ後↓譌｢螳壹・髱偵Μ繝ｳ繧ｯ菴薙∈謌ｻ繧峨↑縺・ｈ縺・√け繝ｪ繧｢蜑阪・繝輔か繝ｳ繝医ｒ險俶・繝ｻ蠕ｩ蜈・☆繧・Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧貞叙蠕・ _
    ByVal src As Range, _
    ByRef fn As String, ByRef fs As Double, ByRef fc As Variant, _
    ByRef fBold As Boolean, ByRef fItalic As Boolean, ByRef fUl As Long)
    On Error Resume Next
    fn = "": fs = 0: fc = Empty: fBold = False: fItalic = False: fUl = xlUnderlineStyleNone
    If src Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    With src.Font
        fn = .Name
        fs = .Size
        fc = .Color
        fBold = .Bold
        fItalic = .Italic
        fUl = .Underline
    End With
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧帝←逕ｨ( _
    ByVal tgt As Range, _
    ByVal fn As String, ByVal fs As Double, ByVal fc As Variant, _
    ByVal fBold As Boolean, ByVal fItalic As Boolean, ByVal fUl As Long)
    On Error Resume Next
    If tgt Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    With tgt.Font
        If Len(fn) > 0 Then .Name = fn
        If fs > 0 Then .Size = fs
        If Not IsEmpty(fc) Then .Color = fc
        .Bold = fBold
        .Italic = fItalic
        .Underline = fUl
    End With
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 遽・峇蜀・・蜷・そ繝ｫ縺ｫ莉倥＞縺溘ワ繧､繝代・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ縺縺大炎髯､・域嶌蠑上・邯ｭ謖・ｼ・Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・謖・ｮ夂ｯ・峇縺ｮ繝上う繝代・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ繧貞炎髯､(ByVal wsMain As Worksheet, ByVal Target As Range)
    Dim c As Range
    If wsMain Is Nothing Or Target Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    On Error Resume Next
    For Each c In Target.Cells
        If c.Hyperlinks.Count > 0 Then c.Hyperlinks.Delete
    Next c
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・A1・橸ｼ壹ヶ繝・け蜀・〒蜷榊燕縺後檎ｵ先棡_縲阪〒蟋九∪繧九す繝ｼ繝医∈縺ｮ繧ｸ繝｣繝ｳ繝励Μ繝ｳ繧ｯ繧剃ｸｦ縺ｹ繧・Public Sub 繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・邨先棡繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医Μ繝ｳ繧ｯ繧呈峩譁ｰ(ByVal wsMain As Worksheet)
    Dim wb As Workbook
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim coll As Collection
    Dim arr() As String
    Dim i As Long, j As Long, r As Long
    Dim n As Long
    Dim temp As String
    Dim sn As String
    Dim afn As String, afs As Double, afc As Variant
    Dim aBold As Boolean, aIt As Boolean, aUl As Long
    Dim srcA As Range
    
    ' 繧ｯ繝ｪ繧｢蜑阪↓ A 蛻励Μ繝ｳ繧ｯ縺ｮ隕区悽繝輔か繝ｳ繝医ｒ險俶・・育┌縺代ｌ縺ｰ譌･莉倩ｦ句・縺・C7・・    Set srcA = wsMain.Cells(2, 1)
    If Len(Trim$(CStr(srcA.Value))) = 0 Then Set srcA = wsMain.Cells(1, 1)
    If Len(Trim$(CStr(srcA.Value))) = 0 Then Set srcA = wsMain.Cells(7, 3)
    繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧貞叙蠕・srcA, afn, afs, afc, aBold, aIt, aUl
    
    Set wb = wsMain.Parent
    Set coll = New Collection
    For Each ws In wb.Worksheets
        If Left$(ws.Name, 3) = "邨先棡_" Then coll.Add ws.Name
    Next ws
    
    ' Clear 縺縺ｨ A 蛻励・繝輔か繝ｳ繝医′譌｢螳壹↓謌ｻ繧・竊・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ蜑企勁・句・螳ｹ縺ｮ縺ｿ繧ｯ繝ｪ繧｢
    ' 邨先棡_* 縺悟｢励∴縺ｦ繧ょ叙繧翫％縺ｼ縺輔↑縺・ｈ縺・A 蛻励・遒ｺ菫晁｡後ｒ蠎・￡繧具ｼ医瑚ｨ育判邨先棡縲崎ｦ句・縺暦ｼ九Μ繝ｳ繧ｯ蛻暦ｼ・    繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・謖・ｮ夂ｯ・峇縺ｮ繝上う繝代・繝ｪ繝ｳ繧ｯ繧貞炎髯､ wsMain, wsMain.Range("A1:A120")
    wsMain.Range("A1:A120").ClearContents
    
    If coll.Count = 0 Then
        wsMain.Range("A1").Value = "・育ｵ先棡_* 繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医↑縺暦ｼ・
        繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧帝←逕ｨ wsMain.Cells(1, 1), afn, afs, afc, aBold, aIt, aUl
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    n = coll.Count
    ReDim arr(1 To n)
    For i = 1 To n
        arr(i) = coll(i)
    Next i
    For i = 1 To n - 1
        For j = i + 1 To n
            If arr(i) > arr(j) Then
                temp = arr(i): arr(i) = arr(j): arr(j) = temp
            End If
        Next j
    Next i
    
    wsMain.Cells(1, 1).Value = "險育判邨先棡・医す繝ｼ繝医∈・・
    繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧帝←逕ｨ wsMain.Cells(1, 1), afn, afs, afc, True, aIt, aUl
    r = 2
    For i = 1 To n
        sn = arr(i)
        wsMain.Hyperlinks.Add anchor:=wsMain.Cells(r, 1), Address:="", SubAddress:="'" & Replace(sn, "'", "''") & "'!A1", TextToDisplay:=sn
        繝｡繧､繝ｳ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・繝輔か繝ｳ繝亥ｱ樊ｧ繧帝←逕ｨ wsMain.Cells(r, 1), afn, afs, afc, False, aIt, aUl
        r = r + 1
    Next i

' 邨先棡_*・郁ｨｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝井ｻ･螟厄ｼ峨・蛟倶ｺｺ_*: 螳滄ｨ薙さ繝ｼ繝峨→蜷後§謇矩・〒蛻励が繝ｼ繝医ヵ繧｣繝・ヨ
' 繝ｻ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺怜・縺・ScreenUpdating=False 縺ｮ縺ｨ縺阪ヾelect 蜑阪↓ True 縺ｫ謌ｻ縺輔↑縺・→ AutoFit 縺悟柑縺九↑縺・％縺ｨ縺後≠繧・' 繝ｻ蜈・・ ScreenUpdating 縺ｯ蠢・★蠕ｩ蟶ｰ
' 繝ｻ蠑墓焚蜷阪・ targetWs・・unPython 遲峨・蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺怜・縺ｫ繧ゅ詣s縲阪′縺ゅｊ縲√え繧ｩ繝・メ縺ｧ隕ｪ繝輔Ξ繝ｼ繝縺ｮ ws 縺ｨ豺ｷ蜷後＠繧・☆縺・◆繧・ｼ・Public Sub 邨先棡繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・蛻怜ｹ・AutoFit螳牙ｮ・ByVal targetWs As Worksheet)
    Dim su As Boolean
    If StrComp(targetWs.Name, SCRATCH_SHEET_FONT, vbBinaryCompare) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    ' 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝茨ｼ丞ｮ溽ｸｾ譏守ｴｰ縺ｯ蟆ら畑蛻怜ｹ・ｼ域凾蛻ｻ繧ｰ繝ｪ繝・ラ・峨・縺溘ａ邨ｶ蟇ｾ縺ｫ EntireColumn.AutoFit 縺励↑縺・    If 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝育ｳｻ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝亥錐縺・targetWs.Name) Then Exit Sub
    su = Application.ScreenUpdating
    On Error Resume Next
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    targetWs.Activate
    DoEvents
    targetWs.Cells.Select
    DoEvents
    targetWs.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit
    targetWs.Range("A1").Select
    Application.ScreenUpdating = su
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ 蟆ら畑: 髱櫁｡ｨ遉ｺ蛻励↓ EntireColumn.AutoFit 繧偵°縺代ｋ縺ｨ蛻励′蜀崎｡ｨ遉ｺ縺輔ｌ繧九◆繧√∬｡ｨ遉ｺ蛻励・縺ｿ AutoFit 縺吶ｋ縲・Public Sub 邨先棡繧ｷ繝ｼ繝・蛻怜ｹ・AutoFit髱櫁｡ｨ遉ｺ繧堤ｶｭ謖・ByVal targetWs As Worksheet)
    Dim su As Boolean
    Dim lastCol As Long
    Dim c As Long
    
    If StrComp(targetWs.Name, SCRATCH_SHEET_FONT, vbBinaryCompare) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    On Error Resume Next
    lastCol = targetWs.UsedRange.Column + targetWs.UsedRange.Columns.Count - 1
    If lastCol < 1 Then lastCol = targetWs.Cells(1, targetWs.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    On Error GoTo 0
    If lastCol < 1 Then Exit Sub
    
    su = Application.ScreenUpdating
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    On Error Resume Next
    targetWs.Activate
    DoEvents
    
    For c = 1 To lastCol
        If Not targetWs.Columns(c).Hidden Then
            targetWs.Columns(c).AutoFit
        End If
    Next c
    
    targetWs.Range("A1").Select
    Application.ScreenUpdating = su
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ: 蛻励碁・螳契蝗樒ｭ疲欠螳・6譎ゅ∪縺ｧ縲搾ｼ域立蜷阪碁・螳契蝓ｺ貅・6譎ゅ∪縺ｧ縲搾ｼ峨′縲後＞縺・∴縲阪・繧ｻ繝ｫ繧定ｵ､閭梧勹繝ｻ逋ｽ譁・ｭ励・螟ｪ蟄励↓縺吶ｋ縲・' 谿ｵ髫・縺ｮ xlsx 蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ逶ｴ蠕後↓蜻ｼ縺ｶ・・penpyxl 蛛ｴ縺ｮ譖ｸ蠑上↓蜉縺医∝・蟷・ｪｿ謨ｴ蠕後・隕九◆逶ｮ繧堤｢ｺ螳溘↓縺吶ｋ・峨・Public Sub 邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_驟榊ｮ悟屓遲疲欠螳・6譎・縺・＞縺医ｒ蠑ｷ隱ｿ(ByVal ws As Worksheet)
    Dim c As Long
    Dim lastRow As Long
    Dim r As Long
    Dim v As Variant
    
    If ws Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    If StrComp(ws.Name, SHEET_RESULT_TASK_LIST, vbBinaryCompare) <> 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    c = FindColHeader(ws, "驟榊ｮ契蝗樒ｭ疲欠螳・6譎ゅ∪縺ｧ")
    If c <= 0 Then c = FindColHeader(ws, "驟榊ｮ契蝓ｺ貅・6譎ゅ∪縺ｧ")
    If c <= 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    lastRow = ws.UsedRange.Row + ws.UsedRange.Rows.Count - 1
    If lastRow < 2 Then Exit Sub
    
    On Error Resume Next
    For r = 2 To lastRow
        v = ws.Cells(r, c).Value
        If IsError(v) Then
            ' skip
        ElseIf Trim$(CStr(v)) = "縺・＞縺・ Then
            With ws.Cells(r, c)
                .Interior.Color = RGB(255, 0, 0)
                .Font.Color = RGB(255, 255, 255)
                .Font.Bold = True
            End With
        End If
    Next r
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 驕主悉縺ｮ蜿悶ｊ霎ｼ縺ｿ荳榊・蜷医〒谿九▲縺溘悟・險ｭ螳喟邨先棡_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ (2)縲咲ｭ峨ｒ蜑企勁・域悽菴薙す繝ｼ繝医・谿九☆・・' 窶ｻ蜻ｼ縺ｳ蜃ｺ縺怜・縺・DisplayAlerts=False 縺ｮ縺ｨ縺阪∫ｵゆｺ・凾縺ｫ True 縺ｫ謌ｻ縺輔↑縺・ｼ医す繝ｼ繝亥炎髯､遒ｺ隱阪′蜃ｺ繧九・繧帝亟縺撰ｼ・Public Sub 蛻苓ｨｭ螳夂ｵ先棡繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ荳隕ｧ_逡ｪ蜿ｷ莉倥″驥崎､・す繝ｼ繝医ｒ蜑企勁(ByVal wb As Workbook)

' 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝茨ｼ医♀繧医・螳溽ｸｾ譏守ｴｰ・峨・陦ｨ遉ｺ蛟咲紫繧定ｨｭ螳夲ｼ亥推繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医ｒ繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝悶↓縺励※ ActiveWindow.Zoom・・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦ｨ遉ｺ蛟咲紫繧定ｨｭ螳・ByVal wb As Workbook, ByVal zoomPercent As Long)

' 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝茨ｼ壼叙繧願ｾｼ縺ｿ逶ｴ蠕後↓蛻怜ｹ・ｒ險ｭ螳夲ｼ・ython 譛ｬ菴薙〒縺ｯ蛻怜ｹ・ｒ譖ｸ縺九↑縺・ｼ・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・蛻怜ｹ・ｒ險ｭ螳・ByVal ws As Worksheet)
    Dim lastCol As Long
    Dim lastHdr As Long
    Dim lastUsed As Long
    Dim lastTitle As Long
    Dim c As Long
    Const HDR_ROW As Long = 3   ' Python 陦ｨ隕句・縺苓｡鯉ｼ・?D 蝗ｺ螳夊ｦ句・縺暦ｼ畿? 譎ょ綾・峨↓蜷医ｏ縺帙ｋ
    
    On Error Resume Next
    ws.Columns("A").ColumnWidth = 12   ' 譌･莉假ｼ育ｸｦ邨仙粋・・    ws.Columns("B").ColumnWidth = 16   ' 讖滓｢ｰ蜷搾ｼ・ython 蛛ｴ繝輔か繝ｳ繝域僑螟ｧ縺ｫ蜷医ｏ縺帙ｋ・・    ws.Columns("C").ColumnWidth = 12   ' 蟾･遞句錐
    ' D: 繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ讎りｦ・ｼ井ｾ晞ｼNO・俄ｦ 謚倥ｊ霑斐＠
    ws.Columns("D").ColumnWidth = 25
    ws.Columns("D").WrapText = True
    ' UsedRange 縺縺代□縺ｨ E 蛻嶺ｻ･髯阪′縲梧悴菴ｿ逕ｨ縲阪→縺ｿ縺ｪ縺輔ｌ lastCol<5 縺ｫ縺ｪ繧翫∵凾蛻ｻ蛻怜ｹ・′莉倥°縺ｪ縺・％縺ｨ縺後≠繧・    lastHdr = ws.Cells(HDR_ROW, ws.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    lastUsed = ws.UsedRange.Column + ws.UsedRange.Columns.Count - 1
    lastCol = lastHdr
    If lastUsed > lastCol Then lastCol = lastUsed
    ' 1 陦檎岼: 譁ｰ蠖｢蠑上・ D1 縺九ｉ蜈ｨ蟷・ｵ仙粋・・-B 繧ｳ繝ｳ繝懊・C 譖ｴ譁ｰ繝懊ち繝ｳ・峨∽ｸｭ髢薙・ C1縲∵立蠖｢蠑上・ A1
    If ws.Range("D1").MergeCells Then
        lastTitle = ws.Range("D1").MergeArea.Column + ws.Range("D1").MergeArea.Columns.Count - 1
    ElseIf ws.Range("C1").MergeCells Then
        lastTitle = ws.Range("C1").MergeArea.Column + ws.Range("C1").MergeArea.Columns.Count - 1
    ElseIf ws.Range("A1").MergeCells Then
        lastTitle = ws.Range("A1").MergeArea.Column + ws.Range("A1").MergeArea.Columns.Count - 1
    Else
        lastTitle = ws.Cells(1, ws.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    End If
    If lastTitle > lastCol Then lastCol = lastTitle
    On Error GoTo 0
    If lastCol < 5 Then
        ws.Columns(5).ColumnWidth = 3
        Exit Sub
    End If
    For c = 5 To lastCol
        ws.Columns(c).ColumnWidth = 3   ' 譎ょ綾繧ｰ繝ｪ繝・ラ・・ 蛻・・・    Next c
    On Error Resume Next
    ws.Activate
    ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = False
    ws.Range("E4").Activate
    ActiveWindow.FreezePanes = True
    ws.Range("A1").Activate
    ActiveWindow.Zoom = 85
    ActiveWindow.ScrollColumn = 1
    ActiveWindow.ScrollRow = 1
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝茨ｼ壹ち繧､繝医Ν縺ｯ邨仙粋繧ｻ繝ｫ蜈磯ｭ D1・・-B 繧ｳ繝ｳ繝懊・C 譖ｴ譁ｰ繝懊ち繝ｳ・峨・1・就1 縺ｯ譌ｧ繝悶ャ繧ｯ逕ｨ縲・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・繧ｿ繧､繝医ΝA1繧貞ｷｦ蟇・○縺ｫ蝗ｺ螳・ByVal ws As Worksheet)
    On Error Resume Next
    If ws.Range("D1").MergeCells Then
        With ws.Range("D1")
            .HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft

        End With
    ElseIf ws.Range("C1").MergeCells Then

' 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝茨ｼ壼魂蛻ｷ縺ｮ繝壹・繧ｸ險ｭ螳壹・xcel 縺ｧ縺ｯ驕ｩ逕ｨ鬆・ｒ螟峨∴繧九→繝励Ξ繝薙Η繝ｼ縺後★繧後ｋ縺溘ａ縲・' ? 蜊ｰ蛻ｷ繧ｿ繧､繝医Ν 1・・ 陦・竊・竭 A3 讓ｪ蜷代″ 竊・竭｡ 菴咏區縲檎強縺・坂・ 竭｢ 讓ｪ 1 繝壹・繧ｸ縺ｫ蜷医ｏ縺帙ｋ 竊・竭｣ 1 譌･縺斐→縺ｮ謇句虚謾ｹ繝壹・繧ｸ縲√・鬆・〒蝗ｺ螳壹☆繧九・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・蜊ｰ蛻ｷ繝壹・繧ｸ險ｭ螳壹ｒ驕ｩ逕ｨ(ByVal ws As Worksheet)
    Dim prevPrintComm As Boolean
    Dim lr As Long
    Dim r As Long
    Dim dayStarts As Collection
    Dim i As Long
    
    If ws Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    If Not 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝育ｳｻ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝亥錐縺・ws.Name) Then Exit Sub
    
    On Error Resume Next
    prevPrintComm = Application.PrintCommunication
    Application.PrintCommunication = True
    
    With ws.PageSetup
        ' ?
        .PrintTitleRows = "$1:$3"
        ' 竭
        .PaperSize = xlPaperA3
        .Orientation = xlLandscape
        ' 竭｡ 菴咏區縲檎強縺・搾ｼ・arrow 逶ｸ蠖難ｼ・        .LeftMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.25)
        .RightMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.25)
        .TopMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.75)
        .BottomMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.75)
        .HeaderMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.3)
        .FooterMargin = Application.InchesToPoints(0.3)
        ' 竭｢ 讓ｪ 1 繝壹・繧ｸ・育ｸｦ縺ｯ閾ｪ蜍包ｼ・        .Zoom = False
        .FitToPagesWide = 1
        .FitToPagesTall = False
    End With
    
    ' 竭｣ 1 譌･・・ 繝壹・繧ｸ邵ｦ繝悶Ο繝・け・域律莉倥ヶ繝ｭ繝・け髢薙・阮・＞蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦後・谺｡陦後′鄙梧律蜈磯ｭ・・    ws.ResetAllPageBreaks
    Set dayStarts = New Collection
    lr = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.Count, "B").End(xlUp).Row
    If lr >= 4 Then
        dayStarts.Add 4&
        r = 5
        Do While r <= lr
            If 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦後°(ws, r) Then
                If r + 1 <= lr Then dayStarts.Add CLng(r + 1)
            End If
            r = r + 1
        Loop
        For i = 2 To dayStarts.Count
            ws.HPageBreaks.Add Before:=ws.Rows(CLng(dayStarts(i)))
        Next i
    End If
    
    Application.PrintCommunication = prevPrintComm
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' planning_core 縺ｮ繧ｬ繝ｳ繝育ｽｫ邱・thin color 666666 縺ｫ蜷医ｏ縺帙ｋ・医ワ繧､繝ｩ繧､繝郁ｧ｣髯､譎ゑｼ・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦梧棧繧帝壼ｸｸ縺ｫ謌ｻ縺・ByVal rng As Range)
    On Error Resume Next
    With rng.Borders(xlEdgeTop)
        .LineStyle = xlContinuous
        .Weight = xlThin

    With rng.Borders(xlEdgeRight)

End Sub

Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦梧棧繧貞ｼｷ隱ｿ(ByVal rng As Range)
    ' xlThick 蜊倡ｷ壹ｈ繧願ｦ冶ｪ肴ｧ繧剃ｸ翫￡繧九◆繧∽ｺ碁㍾邱夲ｼ区ｿ・＞繧ｪ繝ｬ繝ｳ繧ｸ・・xcel 縺ｮ Weight 縺ｯ xlThick 縺御ｸ企剞縺ｮ縺溘ａ・・    Const hlR As Long = 204

Public Function 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・陦ｨ鬆ｭ陦後°(ByVal ws As Worksheet, ByVal r As Long) As Boolean
    Dim a As String
    Dim b As String
    On Error Resume Next
    a = Trim$(CStr(ws.Cells(r, 2).Value))
    b = Trim$(CStr(ws.Cells(r, 3).Value))
    On Error GoTo 0
    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・陦ｨ鬆ｭ陦後° = (StrComp(a, "讖滓｢ｰ蜷・, vbBinaryCompare) = 0 And StrComp(b, "蟾･遞句錐", vbBinaryCompare) = 0)
End Function

' Python 縺梧諺蜈･縺吶ｋ譌･莉倥ヶ繝ｭ繝・け髢薙・鮟貞ｸｯ・郁｡碁ｫ倥＆邏・5pt・・Public Function 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦後°(ByVal ws As Worksheet, ByVal r As Long) As Boolean
    Dim rh As Double
    On Error Resume Next
    rh = ws.Rows(r).RowHeight
    On Error GoTo 0
    If rh > 0# And rh <= 5.6 Then 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦後° = True
End Function

' 繧ｿ繧､繝医Ν繝ｻ繝｡繧ｿ・・?2 陦鯉ｼ峨・陦ｨ鬆ｭ繝ｻ蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦御ｻ･螟厄ｼ晁ｨ育判陦後・螳溽ｸｾ陦鯉ｼ域律莉倥・ A 蛻礼ｸｦ邨仙粋縺ｮ縺溘ａ蛻・A 縺ｫ繧・? 縺檎樟繧後ｋ・・Public Function 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・繝・・繧ｿ陦後°(ByVal ws As Worksheet, ByVal r As Long) As Boolean
    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・繝・・繧ｿ陦後° = False
    If r <= 2 Then Exit Function
    If 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・陦ｨ鬆ｭ陦後°(ws, r) Then Exit Function
    If 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・蛹ｺ蛻・ｊ陦後°(ws, r) Then Exit Function

    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・繝・・繧ｿ陦後° = True
End Function

Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後ワ繧､繝ｩ繧､繝・Clear(ByVal wb As Workbook)
    Dim ws As Worksheet

    If Len(mGanttHL_SheetName) = 0 Then Exit Sub

    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = wb.Worksheets(mGanttHL_SheetName)
    On Error GoTo 0
    If ws Is Nothing Then GoTo ResetState
    
    On Error Resume Next
    Set rng = ws.Range(ws.Cells(mGanttHL_Row, 1), ws.Cells(mGanttHL_Row, mGanttHL_LastCol))
    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦梧棧繧帝壼ｸｸ縺ｫ謌ｻ縺・rng
    On Error GoTo 0
    
ResetState:
    mGanttHL_SheetName = vbNullString
    mGanttHL_Row = 0
    mGanttHL_LastCol = 0
End Sub

' ThisWorkbook.SheetSelectionChange 縺九ｉ蜻ｼ縺ｶ・域ｨ呎ｺ悶Δ繧ｸ繝･繝ｼ繝ｫ縺ｯ Public 蠢・茨ｼ・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後ワ繧､繝ｩ繧､繝・OnSelection(ByVal sh As Object, ByVal Target As Range)
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim wb As Workbook
    Dim r As Long
    Dim lastCol As Long
    Dim rng As Range
    
    On Error GoTo QuietExit
    If sh Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    If Not TypeOf sh Is Worksheet Then Exit Sub
    Set ws = sh
    Set wb = ws.Parent
    
    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後ワ繧､繝ｩ繧､繝・Clear wb
    
    If Not 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝育ｳｻ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝亥錐縺・ws.Name) Then Exit Sub
    If Target Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    
    r = Target.Cells(1, 1).Row
    If Not 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦後・繝・・繧ｿ陦後°(ws, r) Then Exit Sub
    
    On Error Resume Next
    lastCol = ws.UsedRange.Column + ws.UsedRange.Columns.Count - 1
    On Error GoTo 0
    If lastCol < 4 Then lastCol = 4
    
    Set rng = ws.Range(ws.Cells(r, 1), ws.Cells(r, lastCol))
    邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・陦梧棧繧貞ｼｷ隱ｿ rng
    
    mGanttHL_SheetName = ws.Name
    mGanttHL_Row = r
    mGanttHL_LastCol = lastCol
QuietExit:
End Sub

' 譌｢蟄倥ヶ繝・け縺ｧ險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝医′縲後そ繝ｫ縺ｮ譖ｸ蠑剰ｨｭ螳壹咲┌蜉ｹ縺ｮ菫晁ｭｷ縺ｮ縺ｨ縺阪√ワ繧､繝ｩ繧､繝育ｽｫ邱壹′蜉ｹ縺九↑縺・ゅヱ繧ｹ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝峨・ SHEET_FONT_UNPROTECT_PASSWORD 縺ｮ縺ｿ蟇ｾ蠢懶ｼ域焔蜍輔ヱ繧ｹ繝ｯ繝ｼ繝峨・繝ｦ繝ｼ繧ｶ繝ｼ縺御ｸ蠎ｦ隗｣髯､縺励※縺九ｉ螳溯｡鯉ｼ・Public Sub 邨先棡_險ｭ蛯吶ぎ繝ｳ繝・菫晁ｭｷ繧呈嶌蠑剰ｨｭ螳夊ｨｱ蜿ｯ縺ｧ譖ｴ譁ｰ()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim nm As Variant
    
    For Each nm In Array(SHEET_RESULT_EQUIP_GANTT, SHEET_RESULT_EQUIP_GANTT_ACTUAL_DETAIL)
        On Error Resume Next
        Set ws = Nothing
        Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(CStr(nm))
        If ws Is Nothing Then GoTo NextGanttProt
        If ws.ProtectContents Then
            If Len(SHEET_FONT_UNPROTECT_PASSWORD) > 0 Then
                ws.Unprotect Password:=SHEET_FONT_UNPROTECT_PASSWORD
            End If
            If ws.ProtectContents Then ws.Unprotect
        End If
        If ws.ProtectContents Then GoTo NextGanttProt
        If Len(SHEET_FONT_UNPROTECT_PASSWORD) > 0 Then
            ws.Protect Password:=SHEET_FONT_UNPROTECT_PASSWORD, DrawingObjects:=True, Contents:=True, UserInterfaceOnly:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True
        Else
            ws.Protect DrawingObjects:=True, Contents:=True, UserInterfaceOnly:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True
        End If
NextGanttProt:
        Err.Clear
    Next nm
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub

' 繧ｷ繝ｼ繝井ｸｦ縺ｳ・壼倶ｺｺ_*・亥錐蜑肴・鬆・ｼ俄・ 縺昴・蠕後ｍ縺ｫ LOG 竊・譛蠕後↓縲瑚ｨｭ螳壹・' ・医す繝ｼ繝亥錐縺ｯ豁｣遒ｺ縺ｫ LOG / 險ｭ螳壹ら┌縺・ｴ蜷医・繧ｹ繧ｭ繝・・・・' =========================================================
Public Sub 蛟倶ｺｺ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医ｒ譛ｫ蟆ｾ縺ｸ荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺・)
    Dim wb As Workbook
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim arr() As String
    Dim n As Long
    Dim i As Long
    Dim j As Long
    Dim temp As String
    
    Set wb = ThisWorkbook
    n = 0
    For Each ws In wb.Worksheets
        If Left$(ws.Name, 3) = "蛟倶ｺｺ_" Then
            n = n + 1
            ReDim Preserve arr(1 To n)
            arr(n) = ws.Name
        End If
    Next ws
    
    If n > 0 Then
        For i = 1 To n - 1
            For j = i + 1 To n
                If arr(i) > arr(j) Then
                    temp = arr(i): arr(i) = arr(j): arr(j) = temp
                End If
            Next j
        Next i
    End If
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    ' 1) 蛟倶ｺｺ_* 繧呈忰蟆ｾ縺ｸ・域・鬆・ｼ・    For i = 1 To n
        On Error Resume Next
        wb.Worksheets(arr(i)).Move After:=wb.Sheets(wb.Sheets.Count)
        On Error GoTo 0
    Next i
    
    ' 2) LOG 繧貞倶ｺｺ縺ｮ縺輔ｉ縺ｫ蠕後ｍ・医ヶ繝・け譛ｫ蟆ｾ・・    On Error Resume Next
    wb.Worksheets("LOG").Move After:=wb.Sheets(wb.Sheets.Count)
    On Error GoTo 0
    
    ' 3) 縲瑚ｨｭ螳壹阪ｒ譛蠕悟ｰｾ・・OG 縺ｮ縺輔ｉ縺ｫ蠕後ｍ・・    On Error Resume Next
    wb.Worksheets("險ｭ螳・).Move After:=wb.Sheets(wb.Sheets.Count)
    On Error GoTo 0
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

' ・・tep1螳御ｺ・凾轤ｹ縺ｧ縲悟倶ｺｺ_*縲阪鍬OG縲阪瑚ｨｭ螳壹阪・蜑阪・譁ｹ縺ｸ驟咲ｽｮ・・' =========================================================
Public Sub 驟榊床險育判_繧ｿ繧ｹ繧ｯ蜈･蜉帙ｒ蜑阪∈荳ｦ縺ｹ譖ｿ縺・)

' 蜈ｱ騾夲ｼ壹・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧呈款縺苓ｾｼ繧繧｢繝九Γ繝ｼ繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ蜃ｦ逅・' 窶ｻActiveSheet.Shapes(蜷榊燕) 縺縺代□縺ｨ縲∝挨繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医↓蜷後§蝗ｳ蠖｢蜷搾ｼ域里螳壹・隗剃ｸｸ1 遲会ｼ峨′縺ゅｋ縺ｨ
'   隱､縺｣縺ｦ縺昴■繧峨ｒ蜍輔°縺励∵э蝗ｳ縺励↑縺・す繝ｼ繝医′蜑埼擇縺ｫ蜃ｺ繧九％縺ｨ縺後≠繧翫∪縺吶・'   蜈ｨ繧ｷ繝ｼ繝医°繧牙錐蜑阪ｒ隗｣豎ｺ縺励、ctiveSheet 荳翫・繧ゅ・繧貞━蜈医＠縺ｾ縺吶・' =========================================================
Public Sub AnimateButtonPush()
    Dim shpName As String
    Dim shp As Shape
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim candidate As Shape
    Dim firstHit As Shape
    Dim originalTop As Single
    Dim originalLeft As Single
    Dim hasShadow As Boolean
    
    On Error Resume Next
    shpName = CStr(Application.Caller)
    On Error GoTo 0
    If Len(Trim$(shpName)) = 0 Then Exit Sub
    
    Set shp = Nothing
    Set firstHit = Nothing
    For Each ws In ThisWorkbook.Worksheets
        Err.Clear
        On Error Resume Next
        Set candidate = ws.Shapes(shpName)
        If Err.Number = 0 And Not candidate Is Nothing Then
            If firstHit Is Nothing Then Set firstHit = candidate
            If ws Is ActiveSheet Then
                Set shp = candidate
                Exit For
            End If
        End If
    Next ws
    On Error GoTo 0
    
    If shp Is Nothing Then Set shp = firstHit
    If shp Is Nothing Then Exit Sub
    
    originalTop = shp.Top
    originalLeft = shp.Left
    hasShadow = shp.Shadow.Visible
    
    shp.Top = originalTop + 2
    shp.Left = originalLeft + 2
    If hasShadow Then shp.Shadow.Visible = msoFalse
    
    DoEvents
    Sleep 150
    
    shp.Top = originalTop
    shp.Left = originalLeft
    If hasShadow Then shp.Shadow.Visible = msoTrue
    DoEvents
End Sub

' 繝ｻ谿ｵ髫・・乗ｮｵ髫・縺ｮ繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･縺ｮ縺ｿ: BGM・・ounds 驟堺ｸ九・ Glass_Architecture1.mp3 遲会ｼ峨ｒ MCI 繝ｫ繝ｼ繝怜・逕溘らｵゆｺ・凾縺ｯ繝輔ぉ繝ｼ繝峨い繧ｦ繝亥ｾ後↓ close・亥ｮ御ｺ・メ繝｣繧､繝繧医ｊ蜈茨ｼ峨ゆｻ悶・繧ｯ繝ｭ縺ｮ繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･縺ｧ縺ｯ BGM繝ｻ繝√Ε繧､繝縺ｯ蜀咲函縺励↑縺・' 繝ｻUserForm縲掲rmMacroSplash縲阪ｒ繝励Ο繧ｸ繧ｧ繧ｯ繝医↓霑ｽ蜉・域悴霑ｽ蜉譎ゅ・陦ｨ遉ｺ縺帙★邯夊｡鯉ｼ・' 繝ｻMacroSplash_Show 縺ｯ Application.Interactive 繧貞､画峩縺励↑縺・ｼ医げ繝ｬ繝ｼ繧｢繧ｦ繝磯亟豁｢・峨ＭockExcelUI 縺ｯ莠呈鋤縺ｮ縺溘ａ谿九☆
' 繝ｻ譌ｧ迚医〒縺ｯ Interactive=False 譎ゅ↓ UserForm 縺ｮ蜀肴緒逕ｻ縺梧ｻ槭ｋ縺薙→縺後≠縺｣縺溘よｮｵ髫・/2 縺ｮ RunCmdFileStageExecAndPoll 縺ｯ m_macroSplashLockedExcel 繧貞盾辣ｧ縺吶ｋ縺檎樟蝨ｨ縺ｯ蟶ｸ縺ｫ False
' 繝ｻ邨ゆｺ・・繧ｨ繝ｩ繝ｼ譎ゅ・蠢・★ MacroSplash_Hide 縺ｧ Interactive 繧呈綾縺・' 繝ｻ菴懈・謇矩・→繝輔か繝ｼ繝繧ｳ繝ｼ繝峨・ frmMacroSplash_VBA.txt
' 繝ｻ螳御ｺ・・ vbInformation MsgBox 縺ｯ蜴溷援繧・ａ縲∵ｮｵ髫・・乗ｮｵ髫・謌仙粥譎ゅ・繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･譛邨よ枚・句ｮ御ｺ・メ繝｣繧､繝・・acroCompleteChime繝ｻ險ｭ螳・D4繝ｻsounds\*.mp3・集AV繝ｻ螟ｱ謨玲凾 SystemAsterisk・・' =========================================================
Public Function SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled() As Boolean
    On Error GoTo DefaultTrue
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim v As Variant
    Dim t As String
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_SETTINGS)
    v = ws.Range("D3").Value
    If IsError(v) Then GoTo DefaultTrue
    If VarType(v) = vbBoolean Then
        SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled = CBool(v)
        Exit Function
    End If
    t = Trim$(CStr(v))
    If Len(t) = 0 Then GoTo DefaultTrue
    If StrComp(t, "false", vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
        SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    If StrComp(t, "true", vbTextCompare) = 0 Then
        SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled = True
        Exit Function
    End If
DefaultTrue:
    SettingsSheet_IsSplashExecutionLogWriteEnabled = True
End Function

Public Function SettingsSheet_GetCompleteChimeTrack1to4() As Long
    On Error GoTo Def1
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim v As Variant
    Dim n As Long
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Worksheets(SHEET_SETTINGS)
    v = ws.Range("D4").Value
    If IsError(v) Then GoTo Def1
    If VarType(v) = vbString Then
        If Len(Trim$(CStr(v))) = 0 Then GoTo Def1
    End If
    If IsNumeric(v) Then
        n = CLng(CDbl(v))
    Else
        n = CLng(Val(CStr(v)))
    End If
    If n < 1 Or n > 4 Then GoTo Def1
    SettingsSheet_GetCompleteChimeTrack1to4 = n
    Exit Function
Def1:
    SettingsSheet_GetCompleteChimeTrack1to4 = 1
End Function

Public Sub 繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″_繧ｹ繝励Λ繝・す繝･莉倥″縺ｧ螳溯｡・ByVal splashMessage As String, ByVal procName As String, Optional ByVal arg1 As Variant, Optional ByVal arg2 As Variant, Optional ByVal lockExcelUI As Boolean = False, Optional ByVal allowMacroSound As Boolean = False)
    m_splashAllowMacroSound = allowMacroSound
    On Error GoTo EH
    MacroSplash_Show splashMessage, lockExcelUI
    If IsMissing(arg1) And IsMissing(arg2) Then
        Application.Run procName
    ElseIf Not IsMissing(arg1) And IsMissing(arg2) Then
        Application.Run procName, arg1
    Else
        Application.Run procName, arg1, arg2
    End If
    GoTo Finish
EH:
    On Error Resume Next
Finish:
    MacroStartBgm_FadeOutAndClose
    If m_animMacroSucceeded Then
        On Error Resume Next
        MacroCompleteChime
    End If
    MacroSplash_Hide
    m_splashAllowMacroSound = False
End Sub

' 縺九▲縺薙＞縺・・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧定・蜍慕函謌舌☆繧九・繧ｯ繝ｭ
' =========================================================
' 繧ｰ繝ｩ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ驟崎牡繝励Μ繧ｻ繝・ヨ・・reateCoolButtonWithPreset 縺ｮ presetId・・' 1=繝ｭ繧､繝､繝ｫ繝悶Ν繝ｼ 2=繝・ぅ繝ｼ繝ｫ 3=繧ｪ繝ｬ繝ｳ繧ｸ 4=繝輔か繝ｬ繧ｹ繝医げ繝ｪ繝ｼ繝ｳ 5=繝代・繝励Ν
' 6=繧､繝ｳ繝・ぅ繧ｴ 7=繧ｹ繝ｬ繝ｼ繝・8=繧ｳ繝ｼ繝ｩ繝ｫ 9=繧｢繝ｳ繝舌・ 10=繝槭ぞ繝ｳ繧ｿ
Public Function CoolButtonGradientTop(ByVal presetId As Long) As Long
    Select Case presetId
        Case 1: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(65, 105, 225)
        Case 2: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(0, 180, 170)
        Case 3: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(255, 160, 60)
        Case 4: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(60, 179, 113)
        Case 5: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(186, 85, 211)
        Case 6: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(100, 120, 220)
        Case 7: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(130, 140, 150)
        Case 8: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(255, 120, 120)
        Case 9: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(255, 200, 80)
        Case 10: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(230, 90, 180)
        Case Else: CoolButtonGradientTop = RGB(65, 105, 225)
    End Select
End Function

Public Function CoolButtonGradientBottom(ByVal presetId As Long) As Long
    Select Case presetId
        Case 1: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(0, 0, 139)
        Case 2: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(0, 100, 95)
        Case 3: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(180, 80, 0)
        Case 4: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(0, 90, 40)
        Case 5: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(75, 0, 130)
        Case 6: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(40, 50, 120)
        Case 7: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(70, 75, 85)
        Case 8: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(180, 50, 50)
        Case 9: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(180, 120, 0)
        Case 10: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(140, 30, 100)
        Case Else: CoolButtonGradientBottom = RGB(0, 0, 139)
    End Select
End Function

Public Sub CreateCoolButtonWithPreset(btnText As String, macroName As String, posX As Single, posY As Single, ByVal presetId As Long, Optional stableShapeName As String)
    CreateCoolButton btnText, macroName, posX, posY, CoolButtonGradientTop(presetId), CoolButtonGradientBottom(presetId), stableShapeName
End Sub

' 驟崎牡繝励Μ繧ｻ繝・ヨ P1・霸10 縺ｮ隕区悽繧帝・鄂ｮ・医・繧ｯ繝ｭ縺ｯ蜑ｲ繧雁ｽ薙※縺壹∬ｦ九◆逶ｮ遒ｺ隱阪・濶ｲ驕ｸ縺ｳ逕ｨ・・Sub 縺九▲縺薙＞縺・・繧ｿ繝ｳ_驟崎牡繧ｵ繝ｳ繝励Ν菴懈・()
    Dim i As Long
    Dim x As Single
    Dim y As Single
    Const colW As Single = 232
    Const rowH As Single = 62
    Const left0 As Single = 40
    Const top0 As Single = 40
    
    For i = 1 To 10
        x = left0 + CSng((i - 1) Mod 5) * colW
        y = top0 + CSng((i - 1) \ 5) * rowH
        CreateCoolButton "P" & CStr(i), "縺九▲縺薙＞縺・・繧ｿ繝ｳ繧剃ｽ懈・", x, y, CoolButtonGradientTop(i), CoolButtonGradientBottom(i)
        On Error Resume Next
        ActiveSheet.Shapes(ActiveSheet.Shapes.Count).OnAction = ""
        On Error GoTo 0
    Next i
    AppMsgBox "驟崎牡繝励Μ繧ｻ繝・ヨ P1・霸10 縺ｮ隕区悽繧帝・鄂ｮ縺励∪縺励◆縲・ & vbCrLf & _
           "繧ｯ繝ｪ繝・け縺励※繧ゅ・繧ｯ繝ｭ縺ｯ蜍輔″縺ｾ縺帙ｓ縲ゆｸ崎ｦ√↑繧牙峙蠖｢繧貞炎髯､縺励※縺上□縺輔＞縲・, vbInformation
End Sub

' 繧｢繧ｯ繝・ぅ繝悶す繝ｼ繝井ｸ翫↓縲√げ繝ｩ繝・・繧ｷ繝ｧ繝ｳ・区款荳九い繝九Γ逕ｨ縺ｮ繧ｯ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝懊ち繝ｳ繧・縺､驟咲ｽｮ・・nputBox 縺ｧ譁・ｨ繝ｻ繝槭け繝ｭ蜷阪・蠎ｧ讓吶・驟崎牡繧呈欠螳夲ｼ・' 蜑ｲ繧雁ｽ薙※蜈医・縲後い繝九Γ莉倥″_*縲阪↑縺ｩ縲∝・鬆ｭ縺ｧ AnimateButtonPush 繧貞他縺ｶ繝槭け繝ｭ繧呈耳螂ｨ・亥峙蠖｢縺ｫ譛ｬ菴薙ｒ逶ｴ蜑ｲ繧雁ｽ薙※縺吶ｋ縺ｨ繧｢繝九Γ縺ｯ蜍輔″縺ｾ縺帙ｓ・・Public Sub 繧｢繝九Γ莉倥″繝槭け繝ｭ逕ｨ_繧ｯ繝ｼ繝ｫ繝懊ち繝ｳ繧貞ｯｾ隧ｱ驟咲ｽｮ()
